It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for:\+                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation:\+ the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/\+docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization:\+ you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering:\+ the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation:\+ whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. Callable\+[\+[Decorated\+Callable]\+, Decorated\+Callable]\+ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1APIRouter_aa72eb56dd6d209edd1bf859d458969dc}{delete}} (self, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[str, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The URL path to be used for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}. "{}"{}"{}),]\+ path, \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[Any, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for:\+                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation:\+ the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/\+docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization:\+ you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering:\+ the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation:\+ whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1Response}{Response}} Model]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+tutorial/\+response-\/model/\+). If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation:\+ whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error). If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation:\+ whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1Response}{Response}} Model]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+tutorial/\+response-\/model/\+).                "{}"{}"{}),]\+ response\+\_\+model=Default(None), \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[Optional\+[int]\+, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The default \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}} code to be used for the response.                You could override the \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}} code by returning a response directly.                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1Response}{Response}} Status Code]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+tutorial/\+response-\/\doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}}-\/code/\+). "{}"{}"{}),]\+ path, \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[Any, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}("{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for:\+                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation:\+ the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/\+docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization:\+ you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering:\+ the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation:\+ whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error). \doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\begin{DoxyVerb}`APIRouter` class, used to group *path operations*, for example to structure
an app in multiple files. It would then be included in the `FastAPI` app, or
in another `APIRouter` (ultimately included in the app).

Read more about it in the
[FastAPI docs for Bigger Applications - Multiple Files](https://fastapi.tiangolo.com/tutorial/bigger-applications/).

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()


@router.get("/users/", tags=["users"])
async def read_users():
    return [{"username": "Rick"}, {"username": "Morty"}]


app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

For example, in \`{}http:\+/\+/\+example.\+com/\+items\`{}, the path is \`{}/\+items\`{}.                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+}]{path}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Any,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for:\+                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation:\+ the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/\+docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization:\+ you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering:\+ the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation:\+ whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1Response}{Response}} Model]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+tutorial/\+response-\/model/\+).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{response\+\_\+model}{ = {\ttfamily Default(None)}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Optional\+[int]\+,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The default \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}} code to be used for the response.                You could override the \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}} code by returning a response directly. \begin{DoxyVerb}Add a *path operation* using an HTTP DELETE operation.

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.delete("/items/{item_id}")
def delete_item(item_id: str):
    return {"message": "Item deleted"}

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

"{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+}]{path}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Any,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for:\+                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation:\+ the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/\+docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization:\+ you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering:\+ the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation:\+ whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1Response}{Response}} Model]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+tutorial/\+response-\/model/\+). When \`{}True\`{}, default values are omitted from the response.                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1Response}{Response}} Model -\/ Return Type]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+tutorial/\+response-\/model/\+\+\#use-\/the-\/response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+unset-\/parameter).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+unset}{ = {\ttfamily False}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             bool,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                Configuration passed to Pydantic to define if the response data                should have all the fields, including the ones that have the same value                as the default. This is different from \`{}response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+unset\`{}                in that if the fields are set but contain the same default values,                they will be excluded from the response.                When \`{}True\`{}, default values are omitted from the response.                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1Response}{Response}} Model -\/ Return Type]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+tutorial/\+response-\/model/\+\+\#use-\/the-\/response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+unset-\/parameter).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+defaults}{ = {\ttfamily False}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             bool,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                Configuration passed to Pydantic to define if the response data should                exclude fields set to \`{}None\`{}.                This is much simpler (less smart) than \`{}response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+unset\`{}                and \`{}response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+defaults\`{}. You probably want to use one of                those two instead of this one, as those allow returning \`{}None\`{} values                when it makes sense.                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1Response}{Response}} Model -\/ Return Type]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+tutorial/\+response-\/model/\+\+\#response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+none).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+none}{ = {\ttfamily False}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             bool,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                Include this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} in the generated Open\+API schema.                This affects the generated Open\+API (e.\+g. visible at \`{}/\+docs\`{}).                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for Query Parameters and String Validations]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+tutorial/\+query-\/params-\/str-\/validations/\+\+\#exclude-\/from-\/openapi).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{include\+\_\+in\+\_\+schema}{ = {\ttfamily True}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Type\+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1Response}{Response}}]\+,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                Response class to be used for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}.                This will not be used if you return a response directly.                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for Custom \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1Response}{Response}} -\/ HTML, Stream, File, others]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+advanced/\+custom-\/response/\+\+\#redirectresponse).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{response\+\_\+class}{ = {\ttfamily Default(\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1JSONResponse}{JSONResponse}})}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Optional\+[str]\+,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                Name for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}. "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{name}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Optional\+[List\+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1routing_1_1BaseRoute}{Base\+Route}}]\+]\+,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                List of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operations\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} that will be used as Open\+API callbacks. "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{callbacks}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Optional\+[Dict\+[str, Any]\+]\+,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                Extra metadata to be included in the Open\+API schema for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path                operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}.                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for Path Operation Advanced Configuration]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+advanced/\+path-\/operation-\/advanced-\/configuration/\+\+\#custom-\/openapi-\/path-\/operation-\/schema).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{openapi\+\_\+extra}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Callable\+[\+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1APIRoute}{APIRoute}}]\+, str]\+,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                Customize the function used to generate unique IDs for the \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path                operations\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} shown in the generated Open\+API. \begin{DoxyVerb}Add a *path operation* using an HTTP GET operation.

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.get("/items/")
def read_items():
    return [{"name": "Empanada"}, {"name": "Arepa"}]

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

 Callable\+[\+[Decorated\+Callable]\+, Decorated\+Callable]\+ fastapi.\+routing.\+APIRouter.\+head (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             str,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The URL path to be used for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}.                For example, in \`{}http:\+/\+/\+example.\+com/\+items\`{}, the path is \`{}/\+items\`{}.                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+}]{path}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Any,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for:\+                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation:\+ the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/\+docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization:\+ you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering:\+ the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation:\+ whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1Response}{Response}} Model]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+tutorial/\+response-\/model/\+).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{response\+\_\+model}{ = {\ttfamily Default(None)}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Optional\+[int]\+,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The default \doxymbox{\hyperlink{namespacestarlette_1_1status}{status}} code to be used for the response. "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{response\+\_\+class}{ = {\ttfamily Default(\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1JSONResponse}{JSONResponse}})}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Optional\+[str]\+,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                Name for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}. Only used internally.                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{name}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Optional\+[List\+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1routing_1_1BaseRoute}{Base\+Route}}]\+]\+,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                List of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operations\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} that will be used as Open\+API callbacks.                This is only for Open\+API documentation, the callbacks won\textquotesingle{}t be used                directly.                It will be added to the generated Open\+API (e.\+g. visible at \`{}/\+docs\`{}).                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for Open\+API Callbacks]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+advanced/\+openapi-\/callbacks/\+).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{callbacks}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Optional\+[Dict\+[str, Any]\+]\+,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                Extra metadata to be included in the Open\+API schema for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path                operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}.                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for Path Operation Advanced Configuration]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+advanced/\+path-\/operation-\/advanced-\/configuration/\+\+\#custom-\/openapi-\/path-\/operation-\/schema).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{openapi\+\_\+extra}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Callable\+[\+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1APIRoute}{APIRoute}}]\+, str]\+,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                Customize the function used to generate unique IDs for the \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path                operations\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} shown in the generated Open\+API.                This is particularly useful when automatically generating clients or                SDKs for your API.                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs about how to Generate Clients]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+advanced/\+generate-\/clients/\+\+\#custom-\/generate-\/unique-\/id-\/function).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{generate\+\_\+unique\+\_\+id\+\_\+function}{ = {\ttfamily Default(generate\+\_\+unique\+\_\+id)}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Add a *path operation* using an HTTP HEAD operation.

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI
from pydantic import BaseModel

class Item(BaseModel):
    name: str
    description: str | None = None

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.head("/items/", status_code=204)
def get_items_headers(response: Response):
    response.headers["X-Cat-Dog"] = "Alone in the world"

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

"{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{generate\+\_\+unique\+\_\+id\+\_\+function}{ = {\ttfamily Default(generate\+\_\+unique\+\_\+id)}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Include another `APIRouter` in the same current `APIRouter`.

Read more about it in the
[FastAPI docs for Bigger Applications](https://fastapi.tiangolo.com/tutorial/bigger-applications/).

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI

app = FastAPI()
internal_router = APIRouter()
users_router = APIRouter()

@users_router.get("/users/")
def read_users():
    return [{"name": "Rick"}, {"name": "Morty"}]

internal_router.include_router(users_router)
app.include_router(internal_router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

For example, in \`{}http:\+/\+/\+example.\+com/\+items\`{}, the path is \`{}/\+items\`{}.                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+}]{path}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Any,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for:\+                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation:\+ the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/\+docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization:\+ you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering:\+ the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation:\+ whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error). \begin{DoxyVerb}Add a *path operation* using an HTTP OPTIONS operation.

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.options("/items/")
def get_item_options():
    return {"additions": ["Aji", "Guacamole"]}

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

 Callable\+[\+[Decorated\+Callable]\+, Decorated\+Callable]\+ fastapi.\+routing.\+APIRouter.\+patch (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             str,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The URL path to be used for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}. "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+}]{path}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Any,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for:\+                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation:\+ the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/\+docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization:\+ you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering:\+ the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation:\+ whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1Response}{Response}} Model]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+tutorial/\+response-\/model/\+). "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+defaults}{ = {\ttfamily False}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             bool,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                Configuration passed to Pydantic to define if the response data should                exclude fields set to \`{}None\`{}.                This is much simpler (less smart) than \`{}response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+unset\`{}                and \`{}response\+\_\+model\+\_\+exclude\+\_\+defaults\`{}. "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{include\+\_\+in\+\_\+schema}{ = {\ttfamily True}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Type\+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1Response}{Response}}]\+,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                Response class to be used for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}. "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{response\+\_\+class}{ = {\ttfamily Default(\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1JSONResponse}{JSONResponse}})}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Optional\+[str]\+,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                Name for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}. "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{name}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Optional\+[List\+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1routing_1_1BaseRoute}{Base\+Route}}]\+]\+,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                List of \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path operations\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} that will be used as Open\+API callbacks. \begin{DoxyVerb}Add a *path operation* using an HTTP PATCH operation.

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI
from pydantic import BaseModel

class Item(BaseModel):
    name: str
    description: str | None = None

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.patch("/items/")
def update_item(item: Item):
    return {"message": "Item updated in place"}

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

For example, in \`{}http:\+/\+/\+example.\+com/\+items\`{}, the path is \`{}/\+items\`{}.                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+}]{path}{, }\item[{\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{}{, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Any,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                The type to use for the response.                It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for:\+                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation:\+ the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/\+docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization:\+ you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering:\+ the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation:\+ whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error).                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1responses_1_1Response}{Response}} Model]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+tutorial/\+response-\/model/\+). "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{callbacks}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Optional\+[Dict\+[str, Any]\+]\+,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                Extra metadata to be included in the Open\+API schema for this \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path                operation\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}.                Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for Path Operation Advanced Configuration]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+advanced/\+path-\/operation-\/advanced-\/configuration/\+\+\#custom-\/openapi-\/path-\/operation-\/schema).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{openapi\+\_\+extra}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Annotated}{Annotated}}\+[             Callable\+[\+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1APIRoute}{APIRoute}}]\+, str]\+,             \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classtyping__extensions_1_1Doc}{Doc}}(                 "{}"{}"{}                Customize the function used to generate unique IDs for the \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}path                operations\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} shown in the generated Open\+API. "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{generate\+\_\+unique\+\_\+id\+\_\+function}{ = {\ttfamily Default(generate\+\_\+unique\+\_\+id)}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Add a *path operation* using an HTTP POST operation.

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI
from pydantic import BaseModel

class Item(BaseModel):
    name: str
    description: str | None = None

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.post("/items/")
def create_item(item: Item):
    return {"message": "Item created"}

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

"{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{generate\+\_\+unique\+\_\+id\+\_\+function}{ = {\ttfamily Default(generate\+\_\+unique\+\_\+id)}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Add a *path operation* using an HTTP PUT operation.

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI
from pydantic import BaseModel

class Item(BaseModel):
    name: str
    description: str | None = None

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.put("/items/{item_id}")
def replace_item(item_id: str, item: Item):
    return {"message": "Item replaced", "id": item_id}

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}
 \Hypertarget{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1APIRouter_ae149cf231fa0252bacda18acd4eed448}\index{fastapi.routing.APIRouter@{fastapi.routing.APIRouter}!route@{route}}
\index{route@{route}!fastapi.routing.APIRouter@{fastapi.routing.APIRouter}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{route()}{route()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1APIRouter_ae149cf231fa0252bacda18acd4eed448} 
 Callable\+[\+[Decorated\+Callable]\+, Decorated\+Callable]\+ fastapi.\+routing.\+APIRouter.\+route (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{str}]{path}{, }\item[{Optional\+[List\+[str]\+]\+ }]{methods}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{Optional\+[str]\+ }]{name}{ = {\ttfamily None}, }\item[{bool }]{include\+\_\+in\+\_\+schema}{ = {\ttfamily True}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}We no longer document this decorator style API, and its usage is discouraged.
Instead you should use the following approach:

>>> routes = [Route(path, endpoint=...), ...]
>>> app = Starlette(routes=routes)
\end{DoxyVerb}
 

Reimplemented from \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classstarlette_1_1routing_1_1Router_a81bcb77a53e13110c0872e61f31a1a17}{starlette.\+routing.\+Router}}.

It could be any valid Pydantic \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}field\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} type. So, it doesn\textquotesingle{}t have to                be a Pydantic model, it could be other things, like a \`{}list\`{}, \`{}dict\`{},                etc.                It will be used for:\+                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Documentation:\+ the generated Open\+API (and the UI at \`{}/\+docs\`{}) will                    show it as the response (JSON Schema).                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Serialization:\+ you could return an arbitrary object and the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} would be used to serialize that object into the                    corresponding JSON.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Filtering:\+ the JSON sent to the client will only contain the data                    (fields) defined in the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}. If you returned an object                    that contains an attribute \`{}password\`{} but the \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{} does                    not include that field, the JSON sent to the client would not have                    that \`{}password\`{}.                \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} Validation:\+ whatever you return will be serialized with the                    \`{}response\+\_\+model\`{}, converting any data as necessary to generate the                    corresponding JSON. But if the data in the object returned is not                    valid, that would mean a violation of the contract with the client,                    so it\textquotesingle{}s an error from the API developer. So, \doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} will raise an                    error and return a 500 error code (Internal Server Error). \begin{DoxyVerb}Add a *path operation* using an HTTP TRACE operation.

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI
from pydantic import BaseModel

class Item(BaseModel):
    name: str
    description: str | None = None

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.trace("/items/{item_id}")
def trace_item(item_id: str):
    return None

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}

Read more about it in the                \+[\doxymbox{\hyperlink{classfastapi_1_1applications_1_1FastAPI}{Fast\+API}} docs for Web\+Sockets]\+(https:\+/\+/\+fastapi.\+tiangolo.\+com/\+advanced/\+websockets/\+).                "{}"{}"{}             ),         ]\+ }]{dependencies}{ = {\ttfamily None}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}Decorate a WebSocket function.

Read more about it in the
[FastAPI docs for WebSockets](https://fastapi.tiangolo.com/advanced/websockets/).

**Example**

## Example

```python
from fastapi import APIRouter, FastAPI, WebSocket

app = FastAPI()
router = APIRouter()

@router.websocket("/ws")
async def websocket_endpoint(websocket: WebSocket):
    await websocket.accept()
    while True:
        data = await websocket.receive_text()
        await websocket.send_text(f"Message text was: {data}")

app.include_router(router)
```
\end{DoxyVerb}
 \Hypertarget{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1APIRouter_a5f9330167494937a2e1196b21576a303}\index{fastapi.routing.APIRouter@{fastapi.routing.APIRouter}!websocket\_route@{websocket\_route}}
\index{websocket\_route@{websocket\_route}!fastapi.routing.APIRouter@{fastapi.routing.APIRouter}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{websocket\_route()}{websocket\_route()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classfastapi_1_1routing_1_1APIRouter_a5f9330167494937a2e1196b21576a303} 
 Callable\+[\+[Decorated\+Callable]\+, Decorated\+Callable]\+ fastapi.\+routing.\+APIRouter.\+websocket\+\_\+route (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self}{, }\item[{str}]{path}{, }\item[{Union\+[str, None]\+ }]{name}{ = {\ttfamily None}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}We no longer document this decorator style API, and its usage is discouraged.
Instead you should use the following approach:

>>> routes = [WebSocketRoute(path, endpoint=...), ...]
>>> app = Starlette(routes=routes)
\end{DoxyVerb}
